var YSFOVERRIDE = {
    "use": function() {
        var func, args = [], useQueue;
        for(var x=0; x<arguments.length; x++) {
            args.push(arguments[x]);
        }
        if(args.length) {
            useQueue = this.getUseQueue();
            if(typeof args[args.length - 1] === "function") {
                func = args.pop();
                useQueue.funcs.push(func);
            }
            for(var x=0; x<args.length; x++) {
                if(useQueue.requires.indexOf(args[x]) === -1) {
                    useQueue.requires.push(args[x]);
                }
            }
            if(this._INST) {
                this.exec();
            }
        }
    },
    "_currentUseQueue": null,
    "getUseQueue": function() {
        if(this._currentUseQueue === null) {
            this._currentUseQueue = {
                "funcs": [],
                "requires": []
            };
        }
        return this._currentUseQueue;
    },
    "resetUseQueue": function() {
        this._currentUseQueue = null;
    },
    "rotateUseQueue": function() {
        var useQueue = this.getUseQueue();
        this.resetUseQueue();
        return useQueue;
    },
    "_INST": null,
    "requires": [],
    "funcs": [],
    "getInstance": function() {
        var _YSF;
        if(this._INST) {
            _YSF = this._INST;
        }
        else {
            _YSF = YUI();
            _YSF.applyConfig(YUI.YUICfg);
            this._INST = _YSF;
        }
        return _YSF;
    },
    "exec": function() {
        var _YSF, funcs, execFunc,
            useQueue = this.rotateUseQueue(),
            self = this;

        execFunc = function(Y) {
            var func;
            //Y.log(useQueue.requires.join(", "));
            while(useQueue.funcs.length) {
                //Y.log("Executing use(). Remaining: " + useQueue.funcs.length);
                func = useQueue.funcs.shift();
                func(Y);
            }
        };
        _YSF = this.getInstance();
        _YSF.use.apply(_YSF, useQueue.requires.concat([execFunc]));

    }
};


var useYSFOverride = true;
YUI.YUICfg.root='yui:'+ YUI.version + '/';
YUI.YUICfg.comboSep = '&';

if(useYSFOverride) {
    YSF = YSFOVERRIDE;
}
else {
    YSF = YUI();
    YSF.applyConfig(YUI.YUICfg);
}

    League.superclass.constructor.apply(this, arguments);

League.ATTRS = {

    'id' : {
        value : '658258',
        readOnly : true
    },
    'uri' : {
        valueFn : function() {

            var uri = '/f1',
                id = this.get('id');

            if (uri !== '' && id) {
                uri += '/' + id;
            }

            return uri;

        },
        readOnly: true
    },
    'url' : {
        valueFn : function() {

            var url = '',
                uri = this.get('uri');

            if (uri !== '') {
                url = location.protocol + '//' + location.host + uri;
            }
            return url;

        },
        readOnly: true
    }

};

var YSFGlobalPublisher = new Y.EventTarget();

window.onbeforeunload = function(e) {

    var beforeUnloadEvent = YUI.Env.globalEvents.getEvent('ysf:beforeunload'),
        beforeUnloadSubscribers = (beforeUnloadEvent) ? beforeUnloadEvent.subscribers : {} ,
        reason = null,
        s=null;

    for (s in beforeUnloadSubscribers) {
        if (beforeUnloadSubscribers.hasOwnProperty(s)) {
            reason = beforeUnloadSubscribers[s].fn();
            if (Y.Lang.isString(reason)) {
                break;
            }
            reason = null;
        }
    }

    if (reason) {
        if (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            e.returnValue = reason;
        }
        return reason;
    }

};

});

YUI.Fantasy.SpaceIds.getSpaceId = function(subpath) {

YSF.use('event', function (Y) {

    Y.on('domready', function (e) {

            try {

                YAHOO.i13n.SPACEID = '782200994';
                YAHOO.i13n.TEST_ID = '';

                
                var conf = {
                    use_rapid: true,
                    yql_enabled: true,
                    tracked_mods: [],
                    tracked_mods_viewability: ['fantasy-eyebrow-index'],
                    spaceid: 782200994,
                    nofollow_class: ["yfa-link-tab", "ysf-cta-imgur", "yfa-rapid-nofollow"],
                    client_only: 1,
                    test_id : "",
                    keys: JSON.parse('{"spaceid":"782200994","pd":"players","lang":"en-US","mkrt":"US","site":"fullfantasy","sport":"nfl","hashtag":"nfl","pl4":"nfl","pst":"football","pt":"utility","ver":"fantasyphp","navtype":"server","paid":"658258","pstaid":"free","sck":"ffw"}')
                };

                YAHOO.i13n.ywa= conf.ywa;
                YAHOO.i13n.WEBWORKER_FILE = '/rapidworker-1.1.js';

                var ins = new YAHOO.i13n.Rapid(conf),
                    URL_PATTERN = /^https?\:\/\/([^\/?#]+)(?:[\/?#]|$)/i,
                    body;

                // Send nav timing via rapid
                ins.beaconPerformanceData({
                  perf_navigationtime: 2
                },{});

                window.rapidInstance = ins;
                /**
                 * Sends a beacon-click: Use this to track clicks that can't be tracked with regular rapid tracking due to the rapid link hijacking.
                 * How to use: Add this classname to your element: 'yfa-rapid-beacon' and then add your module name: 'yfa-rapid-module-your-module-name-here'
                 * For example, 'yfa-rapid-module-yfa-reg-createleague'.  You can add this to parent elements, such as anchor tags with your custom 'span'-tag type styling inside these,
                 * up to a nesting level five levels deep (the limit is five to ensure speed/responsiveness).
                 * @param event {Event} A dom click event.
                 */
                function handleBeaconClick(event) {

                    var DEFAULT_POS = 0,
                        MAX_LEN = 30,
                        clickParams = {},
                        tg, tgD, tagName, moduleName, match, position, linkName;

                    function getActionable(target) {
                        var MAX_LOOKUPS = 5,
                            el = target,
                            i = 0;

                        while(++i < MAX_LOOKUPS) {
                            if (el.hasClass('yfa-rapid-beacon') || el.hasClass('Beacon')) {
                                return el;
                            }
                            if (el.ancestor()) {
                                el = el.ancestor();
                            } else {
                                return null;
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    tg = getActionable(event.target);
                    if (!tg) {
                        return;
                    }
                    tgD = tg.getDOMNode();
                    tagName = tgD.tagName.toLowerCase();
                    match = tg.getAttribute('class').match(/yfa-rapid-module-([^\s]+)/);
                    moduleName = (match && match.length > 1) ? match[1] : '';
                    match = tg.getAttribute('class').match(/yfa-rapid-link-pos-(\d+)/);
                    position = (match && match.length > 1) ? match[1] : 0;
                    linkName = '';

                    if ((/a|button/).test(tagName)) {
                        if (tgD.innerText) {
                            linkName = tgD.innerText;
                        } else {
                            linkName = tg.getHTML().replace(/<[^>]+>/g, '');
                        }
                    } else if ((/input/).test(tagName)) {
                        linkName = tg.getAttribute('value');
                    }
                    linkName = linkName.replace(/[^\w\s!]/g, ''); // Clean out characters that will not be easily enterable by keyboard into the analytics tool.

                    //Add New instrumentation here to keep backwards compatability for now.
                    if(tg.getData('slk') || tg.getData('sec') || tg.getData('clickParams')) {
                        moduleName  = tg.getData('sec') || '';
                        linkName    = tg.getData('slk') || linkName;
                        clickParams = tg.getData('clickParams') ? JSON.parse(tg.getData('clickParams')) : {};
                    }

                    var href = tg.get('href');
                    var hrefMatches = href && href.match(URL_PATTERN);
                    clickParams.tar = hrefMatches && hrefMatches[1];
                    clickParams.tar_uri = (tg.get('pathname') || '').substring(0, 300);

                    ins.beaconClick(moduleName.substring(0, MAX_LEN), linkName.substring(0, MAX_LEN), position, clickParams);
                }

                ins.init();
                if (Y.Fantasy && !Y.Fantasy.rapid) {
                    Y.Fantasy.rapid = ins;
                }
                body = Y.one('body');
                body.delegate('click', handleBeaconClick, 'button, input[type=button], a:not(.No-Beacon), .Beacon');
                body.all('form input[type=submit]').on('click', handleBeaconClick); // Need separate listener since submit-button clicks don't bubble.

                
                
                //console.log('document_name: ' + "players-Player List");
                //console.log('tracked mods: ' + [  ]);
            } catch (error) {}
    });
});

        <section id="advancedStatsGlossary" class="Mod Thm-inherit No-m W-100">
  <div class="Bd No-p No-bdry Js-submods">
        <section class="Mod Thm-inherit No-mend" id="yui_3_18_1_2_1700797661380_1200">
    <div id="statsearch" class="Bd No-p">
        <div class="statsearchbox Relative">
            <div class="Mbot-lg">
                <input placeholder="Search for a stat" type="search" name="search" class="Input Input-med text Py-lg Fz-sm statsearch W-100" autocomplete="true" id="statsearchtext" data-closeicon="">
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</section>

<script charset="utf-8" language="javascript">
    YSF.use('node', function(Y) {
        Y.on('keyup', viewStats, '#statsearchtext');
        Y.on('click', function() {
            var input = Y.one('#statsearchtext');
            input.set('value', '');
            viewStats(input);
        }, '.statNav');

        function viewStats(e) {
            var input,
            filter,
            listEls,
            statAbbr,
            statName,
            currInput,
            noResultText,
            hasSearchResult = false;

            input = e.target || e;
            inputText = input.get('value');
            noResultText = Y.one('#noResultText');

            filter = inputText.toUpperCase();

            // Loop through all list items, and hide those who don't match the search query
            Y.all('.stat').each(function(currListEl, index) {
                statAbbr = currListEl.one('.stat_abbr');
                statName = currListEl.one('.stat_name');

                abbrTextValue = statAbbr.get('text');
                nameTextValue = statName.get('text');

                if (abbrTextValue.toUpperCase().indexOf(filter) > -1 || nameTextValue.toUpperCase().indexOf(filter) > -1) {
                    currListEl.removeClass("Hidden");
                    hasSearchResult = true;
                } else {
                    currListEl.addClass("Hidden");
                }
            });

            if(hasSearchResult) {
                noResultText.addClass("Hidden");
            } else {
                noResultText.removeClass("Hidden");
            }
        }
    });
</script>

<script charset="utf-8" language="javascript">
  YSF.use('node', function(Y) {
    Y.on('click', function(e) {
      const el = e.target;
      const statList = el.ancestor('li', true);
      const statSection = statList.one('section');
      statSection.toggleClass("Hidden");
      const isHidden = statSection.hasClass("Hidden");

      const arrowDown = "&#xe002;";
      const arrowUp = "&#xe004;";

      const arrowIcon = statList.one('.arrowIcon');
      const arrow = isHidden ? arrowDown : arrowUp;
      arrowIcon.empty();
      arrowIcon.append(arrow);
    }, '#statsList');

    Y.on('click', function(e) {
      var statSection, arrowIcon;
      const arrowUp = "&#xe004;";
      const arrowDown = "&#xe002;";
      const viewAllStats = Y.one('#viewAllStats');
      const shouldExpand = viewAllStats.hasClass("expand");
      const viewAllStatsText = viewAllStats.get('text');

      // text should change to opposite
      const viewStatsInnerText = shouldExpand ? "Collapse All" : "Expand All";
      viewAllStats.toggleClass("expand");
      viewAllStats.set("text", viewStatsInnerText);
      viewAllStats.set("aria-label", viewStatsInnerText);

      // iterate through all list elements...
      Y.all('.stat').each(function(statList, idx) {
        // get section with description
        statSection = statList.one('section');
        arrowIcon = statList.one('.arrowIcon');

        shouldExpand ? statSection.removeClass("Hidden") : statSection.addClass("Hidden");
        arrowIcon.empty();
        shouldExpand ? arrowIcon.append(arrowUp) : arrowIcon.append(arrowDown);
      });
    }, '#viewAllStats');
  });
</script>
    </div>

<script type="text/javascript">

YSF.use('event-hover',  function(Y) {
	var mainNavLis = Y.all('.Nav-h .Navitem, .Nav-h > ul > li');
	mainNavLis.on('hover',
		
		// Mouseover
		function(){
		 	var li_subnav; 

		 	// Add Hover class to nav li
		 	this.addClass('Hover');
		 	
		 	// Add class to li's subnav
		 	li_subnav = this.one('.Dropdown');
		 	if (li_subnav) {
		 		li_subnav.replaceClass('Hidden', 'Hover');
		 	}
		}, 

		// Mouseout
		function(){
		 	var li_subnav;

		 	// remove class from nav li
		 	this.removeClass('Hover');
			
		 	// remove class from li's subnav
		 	li_subnav = this.one('.Dropdown');
			if (li_subnav) {
		 		li_subnav.replaceClass('Hover', 'Hidden');
		 	}
		});
});

YSF.use("node", "event", "ysf-overlay", "ysf-tout", "ysf-cors", "ysf-ads", function(Y) {
    var noteSelector = 'a.playernote[data-ys-playerid]';
    var OVERLAY_NAME = 'react-playernote-overlay';
    var OVERLAY_CONFIG = {"overlayname": OVERLAY_NAME};
    var playerNoteNode;
    var unmount;
    var PLAYERNOTE_AD_POS = "LREC-1";
    var ad_item;
    var tout = new Y.Fantasy.Tout();

    function closePlayerNote() {
        Y.fire("ysfoverlay:close", OVERLAY_CONFIG);
    }

    function onNavigationLoad () {
                        if (window.benji) {
            var position = 'react-playernotes';
            var position_name = position + '-' + PLAYERNOTE_AD_POS;

            // If we've already rendered this ad, we just refresh
            if (YUI.Sports.Ads.isBenjiElementActive(position, position_name)) {
                try {
                    benji.refresh([ position_name ], {
                        duration: 30,
                        limit: 30,
                        tabFocus: {
                            outOfFocusDuration: 3
                        }
                    });
                } catch (error) {
                    // benji broke, oh well
                }
            } else {
                // We need to render it for the first time
                try {
                    benji.render({
                        [ position_name ]: {
                            id: position_name,
                            path: '/22888152279/us/ysports/fan/dt/us_ysports_fan_dt_top_right',
                            size: [[300,250]],
                            region: 'viewer',
                            kvs: {
                                loc: 'top_right'
                            }
                        }
                    });
                } catch (error) {
                    // benji broke, oh well
                }

                // Remember it was rendered for this page load
                YUI.Sports.Ads.registerBenjiAd(position, position_name);
            }
        }         }

    function optOut () {
        Y.Fantasy.rapid.beaconClick('playercard', 'Opt Out', 0);
        Y.Fantasy.Cors('https://pub-api-rw.fantasysports.yahoo.com/fantasy/v2/users;use_login=1/user_experiment_buckets?crumb=fantasy_apis|YZW1iQmUMpM', {
            method: 'PUT',
            headers: { 'content-type': 'application/xml' },
            data: '<fantasy_content><bucket_name>player_card_opted_in</bucket_name><action>opt_out</action></fantasy_content>',
            xdr: {
                use: 'native',
                credentials: true
            },
            on: {
                success: function () {
                    tout.displayTout({
                        "message" : 'Opted out. Refreshing...',
                        "error"   : false
                    });
                    window.location.reload();
                },
                failure: function () {
                    tout.displayTout({
                        "message" : 'Something went wrong. Please try again.',
                        "error"   : true
                    });
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function showPlayerNote (node) {
        var playerId = node.getData('ys-playerid');
        var view = node.getAttribute('data-ys-playernote-view') || 'gamelog';
        if (view === 'notes' || view === 'video') { // Notes and video are old ones no longer supported, so if that, also go to the default
            view = 'gamelog';
        }

        renderNote(playerId, view);
    }

    function renderNote (playerId, view) {
        var allPlayerId = [];
        Y.all(noteSelector).each(function playersNoteItr (note) {
            var playerId = note.getData('ys-playerid');
            if (playerId && allPlayerId.indexOf(playerId) === -1) {
                allPlayerId.push(playerId);
            }
        });

        // Create node if not created
        if (!playerNoteNode) {
            var body = Y.one(document.body);
            playerNoteNode = Y.Node.create('<div id="' + OVERLAY_NAME + '" class="Overlay Atomic Ta-start" data-overlay-name="' + OVERLAY_NAME + '" data-overlay-width="clamp(min(1200px, 100vw), 80vw, min(1300px, 100vw))" data-overlay-height="clamp(min(400px, 100vh), 80vh, min(975px, 100vh))" data-overlay-constrainpage="false"><div id="player-note-content" style="height: clamp(400px, 80vh, 975px); width: clamp(1200px, 80vw, 1300px);"></div></div>');
            body.append(playerNoteNode);
        }
        // Render into node
        unmount = bootstrapPlayerNotes({
            adLite: 0,
            adPosition: PLAYERNOTE_AD_POS,
            closeOverlay: closePlayerNote,
            onNavigationLoad: onNavigationLoad,
            optOut: optOut,
            context: {
                authed: "1",
                env: "prod",
                feedbackUrl: "https://www.research.net/r/Q3NRBZY",
                gameId: "423",
                isPremiumUser: 0,
                leagueId: "658258",
                playerId: playerId,
                playerIds: allPlayerId,
                spaceId: "782204433",
                sportCode: "nfl",
                teamId: 10,
                view: view,
                week: "12",
                featuresById: {"video":true,"feedback":false,"statGroupings":true,"optOut":false,"outlooks":true,"enableEVPlayer":true,"hasLastSeasonStats":true,"hasTwoSeasonsAgoStats":true}            }
        }, playerNoteNode.one('#player-note-content').getDOMNode());
        // Make page not scrollable
        Y.one('body').setStyle('overflow', 'hidden');
        playerNoteNode.setStyle('overflow', 'auto');
        Y.fire("ysfoverlay:open", OVERLAY_CONFIG);
    }

    Y.on('ysfoverlay:overlayclosed', function (e) {
        if (e.overlayname === OVERLAY_NAME) {
            // Remove react component
            if (playerNoteNode) {
                unmount && unmount();
            }

            // Make sure we reset space id
            Y.Fantasy.rapid.setRapidAttribute({
                spaceid: 782200994            });

            // Remake page scrollable
            Y.one('body').setStyle('overflow', '');
            playerNoteNode.setStyle('overflow', '');
        }
    });

    Y.on('ysfoverlay:overlayopened', function (e) {
        // After we've opened, we want to override the yui3 overlay so we don't show a box shadow on focus
        if (e.overlayname === OVERLAY_NAME && playerNoteNode) {
            var parent = playerNoteNode.ancestor();
            if (parent) {
                parent.addClass('No-boxshadow');
            }
        }
    });

    Y.one(document).delegate('click', function (e) {
        e.halt();

        var anchorNode = e.currentTarget;
        showPlayerNote(anchorNode);
    }, noteSelector);

    Y.on('showPlayerNote', function (e) {
        renderNote(e.playerId, e.view);
    });
});
</script>
<script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
YUI.add('ysf-postload', function(Y) {

    Y.namespace('Fantasy');

    Y.Fantasy.PostLoad = {

        initImages : function(id) {
            var el = Y.one('#'+id);
            if (!el) return;
            var images = Y.all('#'+id+' img[realimg]');
            Y.NodeList.each(images, function(node) {
                var realimg = node.getAttribute('realimg');
                if (realimg && node.src != realimg ) {
                    node.src = realimg;
                }
            });
        },

        initOnlineImages : function() {
            var links = Y.all('img.imimg');
            Y.NodeList.each(links, function(curLink){
                var classes = curLink.get('class').split(' ');
                if ( classes[1].indexOf('http://') != -1 ) { 
                    curLink.set('src', classes[1]);
                }   
            });
        },

        initSelect : function(id) {
            var el = Y.one('#'+id);
            if (!el) return;
            el.on('change', function() {
                el.get('form').submit();
            });
        }

    }

}, '', {'requires': ['node']});
</script>

            if(target_location && !e.target.test('a')) {
                if(e.metaKey) {
                        window.open(target_location,'_blank');
                }else {
                    doc = Y.one('document');
                    doc.set('location', target_location);
                }
            }
        };

        bd.delegate("click", linkableHandler, ".Linkable", null);
    });



    if(document.location.href.indexOf("layout=webview") !== -1 || false) {
        var body = Y.one("body");
        body.delegate("tap", function(e){
            var href = this.get("href");
            if(href.indexOf(document.location.protocol + "//" + document.location.host) === 0 && href.indexOf("layout=webview") === -1) {
                href += (href.indexOf("?") !== -1) ? "&" : "?";
                href += "layout=webview";
                this.set("href", href);
            }
        }, "a[href]");
    }

    Y.one(document.body).addClass('Js-yfa-init');
    if(YAHOO.Sports.invitefriends) {
        YAHOO.Sports.invitefriends.init();

    // Extension Finders

        class: 'fp-player-link',

    }];

    setTimeout(function extensionsFinder () {
        EXTENSIONS_CONFIG.forEach(function extensionItr (extensionConfig) {
            if (Y.one('.' + extensionConfig.class)) {
                Y.Fantasy.rapid.beaconClick('browser_extension_installed', extensionConfig.name);
            }
        });
    }, 2000); // Wait 2 seconds

});

<script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript" language="javascript">

/*
 * YAFT [Yahoo above fold time] is a js performance library aims to measure mainly
 * user perceived performance [aft] by utilizing Navigation and Resource Timing APIs.
 * It returns following metrics via its callback function's first parameter object:
 * AFT ( above fold time )
 * VIC ( Visually Complete )
 * costlyResources
 * domElementsCount
 * ttbf: time to first byte
 * domInteractive: the time at which page is interactive
 * modulesReport: the details of each module’s loadTime, coveragePercentage, inViewPort, resources and start time
 *
 * Appending showaft=1 query param to main Fantasy pages in Chrome will allow you to see aft report visually on the page.
 * More at http://yo/yaft
 *
 */


YSF.use("node", "event","event","node-base","event-base", "json", "cookie","base","jsonp","querystring", function(Y) {
Y.later(10, this, function() {
  if (window.YAFT !== undefined) {
    var perfData = {};
    var recordPerfData = function(type, name, value) {
        if (type === 'common') {
            if (!perfData.perf_commontime) {
                perfData.perf_commontime = {};
            }

            if (!perfData.perf_commontime.initialPageLoad) {
                perfData.perf_commontime.initialPageLoad = {};
            }

            perfData.perf_commontime.initialPageLoad[name] = value;

            return true;
        } else if (type === 'user') {
            if (!perfData.perf_usertime) {
                perfData.perf_usertime = {};
            }

            if (!perfData.perf_usertime.utm) {
                perfData.perf_usertime.utm = {};
            }

            perfData.perf_usertime.utm[name] = value;

            return true;
        }

        return false;
    }

    var yaftCallback = function (aftData, error) {
      if (!error) {
        // Send yaft perf data thru rapid
        var aft = Math.round(aftData.aft);
        var timeToVisuallyComplete = Math.round(aftData.visuallyComplete);
        var startRender = Math.round(aftData.startRender);

        if (aft) {
            recordPerfData('common', 'AFT', aft);
            recordPerfData('common', 'AFT1', aft);
        }

        if (timeToVisuallyComplete) {
            recordPerfData('common', 'VIC', timeToVisuallyComplete);
        }

        if (startRender) {
            recordPerfData('common', 'STR', startRender);
        }

        if (window.rapidInstance !== undefined) {
          window.rapidInstance.beaconPerformanceData(perfData);
        }
        perfData = {};
      }
    };

    var modArray = ['sitenav','sitenavsub','yucsHead','UH'];
    [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll(".Mod")).forEach(function(el,i){
       modArray.push(el.getAttribute("id"));
    });

    [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll(".Ad")).forEach(function(el,i){
       modArray.push(el.getAttribute("id"));
    });

    var yaftPreProcess = function() {
          }

    window.YAFT.init({
      preProcess: yaftPreProcess,
      useNativeStartRenderMeaningful: true,
      modules: modArray,
      maxWaitTime: 5000
    }, yaftCallback);
  }});
});

</script>

 <script charset="utf-8" language="javascript">

YSF.use('node', function(Y) {

    var lastOpenedNote = '';

    var showStatNote = function(e) {
        e.halt();

        var popupId     = e.currentTarget.getAttribute('data-stat-note-id'),
            noteToShow  = Y.one('#' + popupId),
            click_x     = e.currentTarget.getX(),
            click_y     = e.currentTarget.getY();

        noteToShow.removeClass('hidden');

        click_x += 20;
        if(click_x > (window.innerWidth - parseInt(noteToShow.getComputedStyle("width")))){
            click_x = window.innerWidth - 2 * parseInt(noteToShow.getComputedStyle("width"));
        }

        click_y -= (parseInt(noteToShow.getComputedStyle("height")) / 2) - 8;

        noteToShow.setXY([click_x, click_y]);

        var arrow = noteToShow.one(".arrow");
        if(arrow && !arrow.hasClass("repositioned")) {
            arrow.setX(arrow.getX() + 7);
            arrow.addClass("repositioned");
        }

        //Make sure last one removed in case the use is
        //opening a new note without closing the first
        Y.detach("close|click");


        if(lastOpenedNote) {
            /* Make sure the last note opened gets closed */
            if(lastOpenedNote.getAttribute('id') != popupId && !lastOpenedNote.hasClass('hidden')) {
                lastOpenedNote.addClass('hidden');
            }
        };

        lastOpenedNote = noteToShow;
        Y.later(5, window, function(){
            Y.on("close|click",  clickAnywhereToClose, document.body, null, noteToShow);
        }, [], false);
    };

    var clickAnywhereToClose =  function(e, noteToClose) {

        noteToClose.addClass('hidden');
        Y.detach("close|click");
    }

    var init = function(e) {

        Y.delegate("click",  showStatNote, "body", ".has-stat-note");

    };

    Y.on('available', init, '#ysf-stat-notes', this);


});

</script>
